1332026-03-08T22:20:48.585356agentmessage-
The `answer.json` has been written at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here is a full narrative of everything the investigation found:

---

## Grafana API Key Authentication & Scope Enforcement — Complete Map

### Architecture Overview

The system has **three distinct layers**:

1. **Token extraction + cryptographic validation** — `apikeygen` / `satokengen` packages
2. **Business-rule validation** — `authn/clients/api_key.go` (`validateApiKey`)
3. **RBAC scope enforcement** — `accesscontrol` middleware + evaluator pipeline

All keys share the single `api_key` SQL table. Service account tokens are rows in that same table with `service_account_id IS NOT NULL`.

---

### Layer 1 — Token Formats & Cryptographic Validation

#### `pkg/components/satokengen/tokengen.go` — Modern token format (`gl…`)
- **Format:** `gl<serviceID>_<32-char-secret>_<8-char-hex-CRC32-checksum>`
- **`New(serviceID)`** — generates random secret, computes CRC32-IEEE checksum of `gl<serviceID>_<secret>`, hashes with `EncodePassword(secret, checksum)` (PBKDF2-SHA256)
- **`Decode(keyString)`** — validates `gl` prefix, splits on `_`, **re-computes and compares CRC32 checksum** before returning; returns `ErrInvalidApiKey` on any mismatch
- **`(*PrefixedKey).Hash()`** — `EncodePassword(secret, checksum)` → the value stored in the DB
- **`(*PrefixedKey).CalculateChecksum()`** — CRC32-IEEE of the key string, little-endian 4 bytes, hex-encoded

#### `pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go` — Legacy token format (base64-JSON)
- **Format:** `base64({"k":"<32-char-random>","n":"<name>","id":<orgId>})`
- **`New(orgId, name)`** — generates random key, hashes with `EncodePassword(key, name)`
- **`Decode(keyString)`** — base64 decode + JSON unmarshal
- **`IsValid(key, hashedKey)`** — re-hashes and compares (constant-time vi
... (truncated)
